My dad took me here to eat today and we've been here millions of times before despite their previous rude service. The food is good, don't get me wrong, but the service is OUTRAGEOUSLY RIDICULOUS. This time was the last straw. When we came in, the tall man who was taking our order had this disgusted look on his face and I can understand that, it was a busy day, but he had taken our order COMPLETELY wrong. When the wrong food came out, they argued that we had ordered wrong and implied that we should settle for what they put out. This blew me away; how can you run a restaurant and expect this from your PAYING customers? If they had only brought out the correct order and accepted they messed up, I would have been okay. However, they did not. Furthermore, the second waiter came out and kept rapidly reading out our order; how is that supposed to help? Anyways, I don't recommend this place and will not be coming back. There are plenty other restaurants to go to for the same quality food.</text>

Their second location.  Not as good as the original.  But still pretty good.  Way bigger and easier to park.  So rarely a line.  You just can't go to the original on weekend or busy hours in weekday.  It's too frustrating between the long lines and impossible parking.

I do not recommend this company for real estate services. I'll start with the pros. The initial account representative has been pleasant and knowledgeable since my enrollment on 9/30/19 and the service posts on my Facebook page 2 to 3 times a week. However, there  have been a lot of cons and I'm stuck in a service paying twice as much my previous service (Market Leader) with much fewer benefits. Since I enrolled, I have had to speak to numerous representatives and have spent numerous hours on the phone trying to get a working Facebook banner, website and IDX integration. I have had to submit the same  requested information to several different people. Currently, I still don't have a working website & I don't have IDX integration so that my listings automatically come into the software to be viewed by prospective clients or to mak marketing materials.
My last phone call was about a week ago, where I voiced my frustrations and asked for a proration of the $1500 that I paid for a 6 month agreement. After being on the phone for almost 2 hours with about 3 different reps, including one male rep who was extremely rude & would not listen, I was offered an extra month of a useless service, compared to my previous service, or $375 of the $1500 back and they would cancel my contract imediately, even though I didn't receive all of the services that were laid out in my contract. I decided to take the extra month to at least get the small benefit of having posts to my Facebook page and maybe a few leads (so far I have only received one bad lead). I would still have to call Market Leader to ask them how I can migrate my domain away from them to another host in order to possibly get my website working.
Overall, 50% of the people you speak to for this company have bad attitudes and poor customer service and are a complete waste of time to talk to. Instead of wasting more hours on the phone with them, I will keep Market Leader so that I have a working website and can market to clients adequately without the frustration and wasted time. Overall, I have wasted $1500 and about 20 hours on the phone.< /review>

< name>
Rory Benedict< /name>
<date>1622267978324</date><Rating>5</Rating>< text>
We finally visited Solvang after a 25 year hiatus. Found peasants FEAST with good reviews on Google and decided to give it a try. A little bit of a wait, but not long, and we were seated outside under an umbrella. My wife and I shared a bottle of Grassini Cabernet and ordered two appetizers: the Cheesy Cauliflower Soup and a serving of Peasants Bacon. Both were absolutely delicious. The soup was dressed with crushed almonds and herb oil and the bacon was a maple glazed thick portion of pork belly. I had the Grotto Burger: a 6 oz smashed patty topped with triple creme cheese, roasted mushrooms, garlic aioli, and crispy shallots all on a brioche bun. It came with a side and I chose the crispy potatoes. Very tasty. Our waitress was perfect and explained that peasants FEAST tries to locally source their food products, from farm fresh vegetables to seafood. Highly recommended!</text>

Finally we get to go out to eat after quarantine and we made the right choice @peasants Feast in Solvang. The online ordering was so simple. We arrived and snagged a table outside(as of now no inside seating.)We called to let them know we had arrived. Our meal arrived to our table in a few short minutes. We enjoyed an excellent dinner at peasants FEAST.  After seeing pictures from others we were interested in the fish and mushroom tacos, which were both unavailable.  The adults ended up getting the carnitas tacos.  Definitely one of the best carnitas tacos I've ever had.  Larger than your typically street taco.  The carnitas had that awesome crisp. Pickled onions nicely cut through the pork.  The tacos were certainly spicy.  Keep this in mind if spice isn't your jam.  Our daughter said her mac and cheese was the best she's ever had (in all her six years üòÇ).

Dining in was easy with online ordering and table service on the patio.  Staff were responsive and polite.  The owner checked in with guests to ensure everyone was happy.  The patio was dog friendly for those who need that.

Seems this is a new restaurant thus the limited number of reviews (as of August 2020).  We highly recommend peasants FEAST.< /text>

< Review>
I love Habit Burger.  This location in San Marcos is great, very open dining room.  Lots of natural lighy. Most of the time it isnt crowded but if it is inside, there is plenty of seating outside.  The burgers itself are great. Menu is relatively simple but enough choices to make everyone happy. It's mostly under $5, add cheese.  I usually get Teriyaki Char.  My boys get a BBq bacon Char.  Such a good deal for burgers.  The additional fries and a drink will increase the price a bit more.  Fries are good here.  There is a choice for sweet potato fries and green beans.  The drinks are fountain drink but they also have their own lemonade or juices that are just good.  I prefer Habit over In and Out anyday due to more choices.< /Review>
